Embedding and optional tracing of raster graphics is also supported, enabling the editor to create vector graphics from photos and other raster sources. Created shapes can be further manipulated with transformations, such as moving, rotating, scaling and skewing.\r\n\r\nhttps://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Inkscape\r\n\r\nYou can support Inkscape!
